function b64encode(s){
  const chars="ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
  let out="";
  for(let i=0;i<s.length;i+=3){
    const a=s.charCodeAt(i), b=i+1<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+1):0, c=i+2<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+2):0;
    const n=(a<<16)|(b<<8)|c;
    out+=chars[(n>>18)&63]+chars[(n>>12)&63]+(i+1<s.length?chars[(n>>6)&63]:"=")+(i+2<s.length?chars[n&63]:"=");
  }
  return out;
}
const py = `import sqlite3
p = "file:C:/Users/kgray/.codex/state_5.sqlite?mode=ro"
c = sqlite3.connect(p, uri=True)
for name, sql in c.execute("select name, sql from sqlite_master where type='table' order by name"):
    print("-- " + name + " --")
    print(sql or "")
c.close()
`;
const b64 = b64encode(py);
const command = `& "C:\\Users\\kgray\\.cache\\codex-runtimes\\codex-primary-runtime\\dependencies\\python\\python.exe" -c "import base64;exec(base64.b64decode('${b64}'))"`;

function b64encode(s){const chars="ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";let out="";for(let i=0;i<s.length;i+=3){const a=s.charCodeAt(i),b=i+1<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+1):0,c=i+2<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+2):0,n=(a<<16)|(b<<8)|c;out+=chars[(n>>18)&63]+chars[(n>>12)&63]+(i+1<s.length?chars[(n>>6)&63]:"=")+(i+2<s.length?chars[n&63]:"=")}return out}
const py = `import json, pathlib, collections, re
ids = {'019f6c06-6dcb-7102-813c-33a77d001361','019f6c81-fc0e-7f20-a5d3-2d8650365b8a','019f6c85-fe74-7862-b2a7-3f24780cb2d6','019f6c9e-5964-7f31-b47e-78344946bce7','019f6d0b-68b7-7a61-bf6f-22095f9b1ede','019f7152-3a02-7bd1-9715-cb895e108b9f','019f71df-dc7a-7641-a39a-625aba79af02','019f71e2-3dcf-76f3-8d0a-2eb6eae88df2','019f71f4-6a13-78e1-a8f6-71f1c052c449','019f72a8-c77b-73a1-8d72-cc5e1a190911'}
paths=[]
for p in pathlib.Path(r'C:/Users/kgray/.codex/sessions').rglob('*.jsonl'):
    m=re.search(r'([0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f-]{27,})\\.jsonl$',p.name,re.I)
    if m and m.group(1) in ids: paths.append(p)
tops=collections.Counter(); payloads=collections.Counter(); response=collections.Counter(); event=collections.Counter(); meta=collections.Counter(); total=0
for p in paths:
    rows=0
    for line in p.open(encoding='utf-8'):
        if not line.strip(): continue
        row=json.loads(line); rows+=1; total+=1
        tops[row.get('type')]+=1
        payload=row.get('payload') or {}
        if isinstance(payload,dict):
            payloads[payload.get('type')]+=1
            if row.get('type')=='response_item': response[payload.get('type')]+=1
            if row.get('type')=='event_msg': event[payload.get('type')]+=1
            if row.get('type')=='session_meta':
                for k in payload: meta[k]+=1
    print(p.name, p.stat().st_size, rows)
print('files',len(paths),'bytes',sum(p.stat().st_size for p in paths),'rows',total)
print('top_types',dict(tops))
print('response_item_types',dict(response))
print('event_msg_types',dict(event))
print('session_meta_keys',sorted(meta))

const patch = "*** Begin Patch\n*** Add File: Codex_Chats/raw_chats/README.md\n+# Native Codex session archive\n+\n+This directory stores the project-associated Codex rollout files exactly as Codex wrote them. The files under `sessions/` and `archived_sessions/` are byte-for-byte snapshots: they are not rendered, normalized, redacted, reformatted, or edited.\n+\n+These files are intentionally different from the readable, sanitized transcripts in `../chats/`. Depending on the Codex version and the individual session, native rollout JSONL can contain system/base instructions, developer instructions, tool calls and outputs, compaction replacements, token and rate-limit accounting, world/session state, reasoning summaries or events, and encrypted reasoning payloads. Encrypted reasoning remains encrypted; this archive does not claim that private chain-of-thought can be decrypted or reconstructed.\n+\n+## Security warning\n+\n+Raw rollouts can contain credentials, personal paths, private content, unreleased project details, and complete tool output. `manifest.json` records potential-secret category counts but never copies the matched values into the manifest. The raw files are not redacted because changing them would defeat byte preservation and could make them unsuitable for native restoration.\n+\n+Do not publish this directory from a public repository. A Git branch in a public repository is public even before a pull request is merged. Make the repository private before pushing raw sessions, and rotate any credential that may already appear in a rollout.\n+\n+## Archive layout\n+\n+```text\n+raw_chats/\n+  manifest.json\n+  session_index.jsonl\n+  sessions/YYYY/MM/DD/rollout-...-<session-id>.jsonl\n+  archived_sessions/rollout-...-<session-id>.jsonl\n+```\n+\n+`session_index.jsonl` contains only the selected project sessions. Each retained line is copied byte-for-byte from the source Codex index. `manifest.json` is generated metadata containing the exact SHA-256, byte count, record count, recorded internal-state categories, and restore path for each rollout.\n+\n+Run a current snapshot and validate it from the repository root:\n+\n+```powershell\n+python scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --dry-run --verbose\n+python scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --verbose\n+python scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --validate\n+```\n+\n+The synchronizer uses the same project classification rules as the sanitized archive and refuses ambiguous or conflicting session IDs. It reads source rollouts and writes copies; it never edits anything under `CODEX_HOME`.\n+\n+## Restore on a new computer\n+\n+Use the same or a newer Codex build. Clone the repository, install Codex, and close Codex completely before restoring. First verify and preview:\n+\n+```powershell\n+python scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py\n+```\n+\n+For a new Codex home that has no `state_5.sqlite` yet:\n+\n+```powershell\n+python scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py --apply\n+```\n+\n+If Codex has already been launched on the new computer, rebuild its derived thread catalog after closing Codex:\n+\n+```powershell\n+python scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py --apply --rebuild-thread-index\n+```\n+\n+The restore verifies every archive hash, copies each rollout back to its native relative path under `CODEX_HOME`, and merges the project session-index lines. With `--rebuild-thread-index`, it moves `state_5.sqlite`, `state_5.sqlite-shm`, and `state_5.sqlite-wal` into a timestamped `CODEX_HOME/restore_backups/` folder. Nothing is deleted. On the next start, Codex rebuilds its derived thread database from all rollout files already present under `sessions/` and `archived_sessions/`, including unrelated local sessions on the destination computer.\n+\n+The restore refuses to overwrite a different rollout or index entry by default. `--overwrite-existing` exists for a manually reviewed same-ID conflict; do not use it casually.\n+\n+## Compatibility boundary\n+\n+The native rollout files are the durable source records. `state_5.sqlite` is a derived, version-specific thread catalog and is therefore not copied into Git. This restore path was validated against the current local Codex storage contract: Codex scans native rollout files to backfill a missing state database, and the CLI supports resuming a saved session by UUID. OpenAI's public Codex documentation does not currently describe a supported cross-machine chat-import command, so future Codex versions may require an updated restore procedure.\n+\n+An active conversation grows while work continues. A snapshot contains every complete JSONL record present when it was copied; tool results and the final assistant message created afterward can only be captured by the next snapshot.\n*** Update File: Codex_Chats/README.md\n@@\n # Project conversation archive\n \n This directory preserves the visible, project-specific history needed to continue Forever Treasure Companion work across machines. `manifest.json` is the authoritative mapping from a stable source conversation ID to exactly one readable Markdown transcript in `chats/`.\n+\n+Native, unmodified Codex rollout snapshots and the cross-machine restore workflow live in [`raw_chats/`](raw_chats/README.md). Those files can contain secrets and private internal state and must not be pushed while this repository is public.\n*** Add File: scripts/tests/test_raw_codex_chats.py\n+from __future__ import function b64encode(s){const chars="ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";let out="";for(let i=0;i<s.length;i+=3){const a=s.charCodeAt(i),b=i+1<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+1):0,c=i+2<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+2):0,n=(a<<16)|(b<<8)|c;out+=chars[(n>>18)&63]+chars[(n>>12)&63]+(i+1<s.length?chars[(n>>6)&63]:"=")+(i+2<s.length?chars[n&63]:"=")}return out}
const py=`import subprocess, os, json, pathlib, threading, queue, time
root=pathlib.Path.cwd(); exe=root/'tmp-codex-runtime'/'codex.exe'; home=root/'tmp-codex-runtime'/'restore-home'
env=os.environ.copy(); env['CODEX_HOME']=str(home)
p=subprocess.Popen([str(exe),'app-server','--stdio'],cwd=str(root),env=env,stdin=subprocess.PIPE,stdout=subprocess.PIPE,stderr=subprocess.PIPE,text=True,bufsize=1)
q=queue.Queue()
def reader():
 for line in p.stdout: q.put(line)
threading.Thread(target=reader,daemon=True).start()
def send(obj):
 p.stdin.write(json.dumps(obj,separators=(',',':'))+'\\n'); p.stdin.flush()
def response(wanted,timeout=60):
 end=time.time()+timeout
 while time.time()<end:
  try: line=q.get(timeout=min(1,end-time.time()))
  except queue.Empty: continue
  try: obj=json.loads(line)
  except json.JSONDecodeError: continue
  if obj.get('id')==wanted: return obj
 raise TimeoutError(wanted)
send({'id':1,'method':'initialize','params':{'clientInfo':{'name':'raw-restore-verifier','version':'1.0'},'capabilities':{'experimentalApi':True}}})
r1=response(1)
send({'method':'initialized','params':{}})
send({'id':2,'method':'thread/list','params':{'limit':100,'sourceKinds':['vscode'],'useStateDbOnly':True}})
r2=response(2)
rows=(r2.get('result') or {}).get('data',[])
print('initialize','error' if r1.get('error') else 'ok')
print('thread_list','error' if r2.get('error') else 'ok')
if r2.get('error'): print('error_message',r2['error'].get('message'))
print('thread_count',len(rows))
print('thread_ids',','.join(sorted(str(r.get('id')) for r in rows)))
p.terminate()
try: p.wait(timeout=10)
except subprocess.TimeoutExpired: p.kill(); p.wait()
print('state_db_exists',(home/'state_5.sqlite').exists())
`;

function b64encode(s){const chars="ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";let out="";for(let i=0;i<s.length;i+=3){const a=s.charCodeAt(i),b=i+1<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+1):0,c=i+2<s.length?s.charCodeAt(i+2):0,n=(a<<16)|(b<<8)|c;out+=chars[(n>>18)&63]+chars[(n>>12)&63]+(i+1<s.length?chars[(n>>6)&63]:"=")+(i+2<s.length?chars[n&63]:"=")}return out}

first_user_message = ?, preview = ?, has_user_event = ? \"\n+                    \"WHERE id = ?\",\n+                    (*replacement, session_id),\n+                )\n+                changed += 1\n+        connection.commit()\n+        return changed\n+    except sqlite3.DatabaseError as exc:\n+        connection.rollback()\n+        raise RestoreError(f\"Cannot repair Codex's derived thread catalog: {exc}\") from exc\n+    finally:\n+        connection.close()\n+\n+\n+def resolve_codex_executable(value: Path | None) -> str:\n+    if value is not None:\n+        executable = value.expanduser().resolve()\n+        if not executable.is_file():\n+            raise RestoreError(f\"Codex executable not found: {executable}\")\n+        return str(executable)\n+    discovered = shutil.which(\"codex\") or shutil.which(\"codex.exe\")\n+    if not discovered:\n+        raise RestoreError(\n+            \"Cannot find the Codex CLI. Pass --codex-executable with the installed codex executable path.\"\n+        )\n+    return discovered\n+\n+\n+def _wait_for_response(\n+    process: subprocess.Popen[str], responses: queue.Queue[dict[str, Any]], request_id: int, timeout: float\n+) -> dict[str, Any]:\n+    deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout\n+    while time.monotonic() < deadline:\n+        if process.poll() is not None:\n+            raise RestoreError(f\"Codex app-server stopped unexpectedly with exit code {process.returncode}\")\n+        try:\n+            message = responses.get(timeout=min(0.25, max(0.01, deadline - time.monotonic())))\n+        except queue.Empty:\n+            continue\n+        if message.get(\"id\") == request_id:\n+            if message.get(\"error\"):\n+                raise RestoreError(f\"Codex app-server request failed: {message['error']}\")\n+            result = message.get(\"result\")\n+            return result if isinstance(result, dict) else {}\n+    raise RestoreError(f\"Timed out waiting for Codex app-server request {request_id}\")\n+\n+\n+def list_threads_with_codex(executable: str, home: Path, timeout: float = 60.0) -> set[str]:\n+    environment = os.environ.copy()\n+    environment[\"CODEX_HOME\"] = str(home)\n+    process = subprocess.Popen(\n+        [executable, \"app-server\", \"--stdio\"],\n+        stdin=subprocess.PIPE,\n+        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,\n+        stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL,\n+        text=True,\n+        encoding=\"utf-8\",\n+        errors=\"replace\",\n+        env=environment,\n+    )\n+    responses: queue.Queue[dict[str, Any]] = queue.Queue()\n+\n+    def read_responses() -> None:\n+        assert process.stdout is not None\n+        for line in process.stdout:\n+            try:\n+                message = json.loads(line)\n+            except json.JSONDecodeError:\n+                continue\n+            if isinstance(message, dict):\n+                responses.put(message)\n+\n+    reader = threading.Thread(target=read_responses, daemon=True)\n+    reader.start()\n+\n+    def send(message: dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n+        if process.stdin is None:\n+            raise RestoreError(\"Codex app-server input stream is unavailable\")\n+        process.stdin.write(json.dumps(message, separators=(\",\", \":\")) + \"\\n\")\n+        process.stdin.flush()\n+\n+    try:\n+        send(\n+            {\n+                \"id\": 1,\n+                \"method\": \"initialize\",\n+                \"params\": {\n+                    \"clientInfo\": {\"name\": \"raw-chat-restore-verifier\", \"version\": \"1.0\"},\n+                    \"capabilities\": {\"experimentalApi\": True},\n+                },\n+            }\n+        )\n+        _wait_for_response(process, responses, 1, timeout)\n+        send({\"method\": \"initialized\", \"params\": {}})\n+        thread_ids: set[str] = set()\n+        cursor: str | None = None\n+        request_id = 2\n+        while True:\n+            params: dict[str, Any] = {\"limit\": 100, \"useStateDbOnly\": True}\n+            if cursor:\n+                params[\"cursor\"] = cursor\n+            send({\"id\": request_id, \"method\": \"thread/list\", \"params\": params})\n+            result = _wait_for_response(process, responses, request_id, timeout)\n+            for thread in result.get(\"data\") or []:\n+                if isinstance(thread, dict) and thread.get(\"id\"):\n+                    thread_ids.add(str(thread[\"id\"]))\n+            next_cursor = result.get(\"nextCursor\")\n+            if not isinstance(next_cursor, str) or not next_cursor:\n+                break\n+            cursor = next_cursor\n+            request_id += 1\n+        return thread_ids\n+    finally:\n+        if process.stdin:\n+            process.stdin.close()\n+        process.terminate()\n+        try:\n+            process.wait(timeout=5)\n+        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n+            process.kill()\n+            process.wait(timeout=5)\n+\n+\n+def materialize_thread_index(\n+    home: Path,\n+    verified: list[tuple[dict[str, Any], Path, bytes]],\n+    codex_executable: str,\n+) -> dict[str, Any]:\n+    # The first startup makes Codex build its version-specific derived database.\n+    list_threads_with_codex(codex_executable, home)\n+    backup = copy_state_database_backup(home, \"before-metadata-repair\")\n+    repaired = repair_derived_thread_metadata(home, verified)\n+    listed = list_threads_with_codex(codex_executable, home)\n+    expected = {str(entry[\"session_id\"]) for entry, _source, _data in verified}\n+    missing = sorted(expected - listed)\n+    if missing:\n+        raise RestoreError(\"Codex thread/list did not return restored sessions: \" + \", \".join(missing))\n+    return {\n+        \"derived_metadata_rows_repaired\": repaired,\n+        \"materialized_state_database_backup\": str(backup),\n+        \"verified_thread_ids\": sorted(expected),\n+    }\n@@\n def restore(\n@@\n     rebuild_thread_index: bool,\n     overwrite_existing: bool,\n+    materialize_index: bool = False,\n+    codex_executable: Path | None = None,\n ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n     manifest, verified = load_archive(archive)\n     home = home.expanduser().resolve()\n+    executable: str | None = None\n+    if [{"text": "Script completed\nWall time 0.3 seconds\nOutput:\n", "type": "input_text"}, {"text": "Exit code: 0\nWall time: 0.3 seconds\nOutput:\n# Native Codex session archive\n\nThis directory stores the project-associated Codex rollout files exactly as Codex wrote them. The files under `sessions/` and `archived_sessions/` are byte-for-byte snapshots: they are not rendered, normalized, redacted, reformatted, or edited.\n\nThese files are intentionally different from the readable, sanitized transcripts in `../chats/`. Depending on the Codex version and the individual session, native rollout JSONL can contain system/base instructions, developer instructions, tool calls and outputs, compaction replacements, token and rate-limit accounting, world/session state, reasoning summaries or events, and encrypted reasoning payloads. Encrypted reasoning remains encrypted; this archive does not claim that private chain-of-thought can be decrypted or reconstructed.\n\n## Security warning\n\nRaw rollouts can contain credentials, personal paths, private content, unreleased project details, and complete tool output. `manifest.json` records potential-secret category counts but never copies the matched values into the manifest. The raw files are not redacted because changing them would defeat byte preservation and could make them unsuitable for native restoration.\n\nDo not publish this directory from a public repository. A Git branch in a public repository is public even before a pull request is merged. Make the repository private before pushing raw sessions, and rotate any credential that may already appear in a rollout.\n\n## Archive layout\n\n```text\nraw_chats/\n  manifest.json\n  session_index.jsonl\n  sessions/YYYY/MM/DD/rollout-...-<session-id>.jsonl\n  archived_sessions/rollout-...-<session-id>.jsonl\n```\n\n`session_index.jsonl` contains only the selected project sessions. Each retained line is copied byte-for-byte from the source Codex index. `manifest.json` is generated metadata containing the exact SHA-256, byte count, record count, recorded internal-state categories, and restore path for each rollout.\n\nRun a current snapshot and validate it from the repository root:\n\n```powershell\npython scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --dry-run --verbose\npython scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --verbose\npython scripts/sync_raw_codex_chats.py --validate\n```\n\nThe synchronizer uses the same project classification rules as the sanitized archive and refuses ambiguous or conflicting session IDs. It reads source rollouts and writes copies; it never edits anything under `CODEX_HOME`.\n\n## Restore on a new computer\n\nUse the same or a newer Codex build. Clone the repository, install Codex, and close Codex completely before restoring. First verify and preview:\n\n```powershell\npython scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py\n```\n\nFor a new Codex home that has no `state_5.sqlite` yet:\n\n```powershell\npython scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py --apply\n```\n\nIf Codex has already been launched on the new computer, rebuild its derived thread catalog after closing Codex:\n\n```powershell\npython scripts/restore_raw_codex_chats.py --apply --rebuild-thread-index\n```\n\nThe restore verifies every archive hash, copies each rollout back to its native relative path under `CODEX_HOME`, and merges the project session-index lines. With `--rebuild-thread-index`, it moves `state_5.sqlite`, `state_5.sqlite-shm`, and `state_5.sqlite-wal` into a timestamped `CODEX_HOME/restore_backups/` folder. Nothing is deleted. On the next start, Codex rebuilds its derived thread database from all rollout files already present under `sessions/` and `archived_sessions/`, including unrelated local sessions on the destination computer.\n\nThe restore refuses to overwrite a different rollout or index entry by default. `--overwrite-existing` exists for a manually reviewed same-ID conflict; do not use it casually.\n\n## Compatibility boundary\n\nThe native rollout files are the durable source records. `state_5.sqlite` is a derived, version-specific thread catalog and is therefore not copied into Git. This restore path was validated against the current local Codex storage contract: Codex scans native rollout files to backfill a missing state database, and the CLI supports resuming a saved session by UUID. OpenAI's public Codex documentation does not currently describe a supported cross-machine chat-import command, so future Codex versions may require an updated restore procedure.\n\nAn active conversation grows while work continues. A snapshot contains every complete JSONL record present when it was copied; tool results and the final assistant message created afterward can only be captured by the next snapshot.\n", "type": "input_text"}]
